# UI Audit

Generated from the codebase on 2026-04-01T08:54:38.590Z.

## Repo Summary

- Authored stylesheet files found: 52
- Unimported stylesheet files: 6
- Source files with inline styles: 53
- Global stylesheet: Yes - `src/styles/global.css` (loaded in `src/main.jsx`)
- Other root-loaded global files: `src/styles/theme.css`, `src/styles/variables.css`, `src/styles/design-system.css`, `src/styles/responsive-contract.css`, `src/styles/GeneratePromptBar.css`

## CSS Methodology

- Primary styling approach: plain CSS files imported into React components/pages plus a single SCSS file in admin moderation (`src/admin/pages/AdminModeration/AdminModeration.scss`).
- No CSS Modules detected.
- No Chakra UI component usage found in `src/` even though the dependency exists in `package.json`.
- No `styled-components` or `@emotion/styled` usage found in `src/` even though Emotion is installed.
- A `tailwind.config.js` file exists, but no Tailwind stylesheet import/directive was found. Tailwind-like utility class strings still appear in a handful of admin components, so the repo reads as CSS/SCSS + inline styles with some dormant utility-class remnants rather than an active Tailwind system.
- Inline React styles are active in multiple sections, especially generate, calendar, org, and admin components.

### Inconsistencies Flagged

- Theme and token sources overlap: `src/styles/theme.css` uses `[data-theme]`, `src/styles/global.css` uses `html.dark`, `src/styles/variables.css` still contains `.dark`, and `src/styles/design-system.css` relies on `@media (prefers-color-scheme: dark)` overrides. The app has one runtime theme controller but several competing CSS activation patterns.
- Unimported or likely legacy stylesheet files are still present: `src/admin/pages/AdminModeration/AdminModeration.scss`, `src/index.css`, `src/pages/Auth/Login.css`, `src/styles/Navbar.css`, `src/styles/PostCard.css`, `src/styles/Sidebar.css`.
- Cross-section primitives like generic cards, buttons, status badges, typography tokens, and layout helpers are split across `global.css`, `App.css`, `variables.css`, and `design-system.css` instead of a single canonical primitive layer.

## Public & Entry

- Source files with inline styles in this section: `src/pages/Auth/CompleteSignupPage.jsx`, `src/pages/Auth/Login.jsx`, `src/pages/Auth/Register.jsx`, `src/pages/Landing/LandingPage.jsx`

### Component Inventory

No reusable UI components matched the audit heuristics for this section.

### Inconsistencies Flagged

- Landing runs on its own marketing typography and palette (`DM Sans` + `Syne` in `src/pages/Landing/LandingPage.css`) while auth and invitation screens use the product stack (`Manrope` + `Sora`). The handoff from marketing to product is visually distinct rather than unified.
- Public/auth spacing and component rhythms are page-scoped instead of primitive-based, so cards, hero pills, and auth form controls do not share a reusable button/card foundation with the personal app.

- Source files with inline styles in this section: `src/components/BrandKit/AssetUploader.jsx`, `src/components/BrandKit/BrandKitDashboard.jsx`, `src/components/BrandKit/BrandKitExtractLoader.jsx`, `src/components/BrandKit/BrandKitLivePreview.jsx`, `src/components/Dashboard/RealtimeKPICards.jsx`, `src/components/Generate/BatchGenerationGrid.jsx`, `src/components/Generate/GenerationCanvas.jsx`, `src/components/Generate/GenerationPromptBar.jsx`, `src/components/Generate/ImageEditPanel.jsx`, `src/components/Generate/PostProductionPanel.jsx`, `src/components/Generate/PromptSuggestions.jsx`, `src/components/Generate/SEOPanel.jsx`, `src/components/Generate/SessionHistoryRail.jsx`, `src/components/Generate/VideoProcessingModal.jsx`, `src/components/User/ProfileMenu.jsx`, `src/pages/CalendarPage/components/CalendarGrid.jsx`, `src/pages/CalendarPage/components/DraftsSidebar.jsx`, `src/pages/CalendarPage/components/GhostSlotCard.jsx`, `src/pages/CalendarPage/components/OptimalTimesPanel.jsx`, `src/pages/CalendarPage/components/PostCard.jsx`, `src/pages/CalendarPage/components/ScheduleModal.jsx`, `src/pages/Dashboard/UserDashboard.jsx`, `src/pages/LibraryPage/LibraryPageV2.jsx`, `src/pages/Settings/components/AccountHealthModal.jsx`, `src/pages/Settings/components/ConnectedAccountCard.jsx`, `src/pages/Settings/components/MockOAuthScreen.jsx`, `src/pages/Settings/components/PlatformGrid.jsx`

### Inconsistencies Flagged

- Personal surfaces split into multiple visual systems: dark dashboard/generate (`src/styles/UserDashboard.css`, `src/styles/GenerateV2.css`), light utility pages (`src/styles/CalendarV2.css`, `src/styles/LibraryV2.css`, `src/styles/Settings.css`), and a separate Brand Kit system (`src/styles/BrandKit.css` plus `--bk-*` tokens).
- Buttons, cards, and modals are largely page-specific. Dashboard, generate, calendar, settings, connected accounts, and brand kit each define their own interaction patterns instead of sharing one reusable primitive set.
- Generate and calendar components rely heavily on inline styles for progress bars, spacing, and ad-hoc layout tweaks, which makes token drift harder to control.

## Organization Surfaces

- Source files with inline styles in this section: `src/org/admin/BrandKitPage.jsx`, `src/org/admin/CreditManagementPage.jsx`, `src/org/components/calendar/CalendarTimelineView.jsx`, `src/org/components/ContextCard.jsx`, `src/org/components/FolderCreateModal.jsx`, `src/org/components/FolderTree.jsx`, `src/org/components/OrgAccountCard.jsx`, `src/org/components/tasks/TaskBoardView.jsx`, `src/org/components/tasks/TaskTableView.jsx`, `src/org/pages/OrgCalendar.jsx`

### Inconsistencies Flagged

- Organization UI has its own `--org-*` token family and spreads reusable surface styles across `OrgWorkspace.css`, `OrgCalendar.css`, `Pipeline.css`, `PipelineBoard.css`, `CommonRoom.css`, `AssetLibrary.css`, `MyWorkspace.css`, `MyOffice.css`, `OrgGenerateComposer.css`, and `OrgAdmin.css`.
- The same UI element type is restyled per feature. Cards, timeline panels, modals, task boards, folder controls, and admin forms each define their own radius, shadow, and spacing language instead of one org-wide primitive contract.
- Inline styles are active in folders, tasks, account cards, context cards, and timeline views, so part of the org experience bypasses the org stylesheet token system.

## Platform Admin

- Source files with inline styles in this section: `src/admin/components/ContentManager/ContentDataGrid.jsx`, `src/admin/components/ContentModeration/PreviewPane.jsx`, `src/admin/components/ContentModeration/UploadWizard.jsx`, `src/admin/components/KpiCard/KpiCard.jsx`, `src/admin/components/ScoreCard/ScoreCard.jsx`, `src/admin/components/UserDetailsPanel/SocialMediaTile.jsx`, `src/admin/components/UserDetailsPanel/UserDetailsPanel.jsx`, `src/admin/pages/AdminAccountsPage.jsx`, `src/admin/pages/AdminComplaintDetailPage.jsx`, `src/admin/pages/AdminLogsPage.jsx`, `src/admin/pages/AdminModeration/AdminModerationWorkspace.jsx`

### Inconsistencies Flagged

- Platform admin styling is split between `AdminShell.css`, `AdminWorkspace.css`, `AdminDashboard.css`, `AdminAccounts.css`, `AdminModerationPage.css`, and `CreateOrgPanel.css`, with overlapping panel, badge, button, and table patterns.
- Legacy moderation SCSS is still in the repo as `src/admin/pages/AdminModeration/AdminModeration.scss`, but the live moderation screen imports `AdminModerationPage.css`. That duplication increases maintenance risk.
- Tailwind-like utility class strings appear in admin components without a confirmed Tailwind stylesheet import: `src/admin/components/ContentManager/ContentDataGrid.jsx`, `src/admin/components/ContentManager/ContentManager.jsx`, `src/admin/components/ContentModeration/EditModal.jsx`, `src/admin/components/ContentModeration/ModerationQueue.jsx`, `src/admin/components/UserDetailsPanel/UserDetailsPanel.jsx`, `src/admin/components/UserListPanel/UserListPanel.jsx`.
